Authors

The Galaxy Zoo: Mergers project is grateful for the contributions of all of our Citizen Science volunteers. More than 6000 users contributed to the project by running and reviewing simulations or by participating in Merger Wars. It is a Zooniverse tradition to recognize their contributions as co-authors, and we gladly support that tradition. These volunteers are recognized by using the name they provided with their Zooniverse accounts.
